  --- Ralph 344: Breakthrough DFS вАФ Algebraic/p-adic/Combinatorial ---

  в≠Рв≠Р ќµ_Q(вИЪ6) = (вИЪ2+вИЪ3)¬≤ вАФ unique squarefree semiprime! #163

     вЖТ SвВВ(6,2)=31=2вБµ-1=MвВЕ (Mersenne prime!)

     вЖТ F(5)=5 is Fibonacci fixed point. sopfr(6)=5
     вЖТ F(k)=k only for kвИИ{1,5}. sopfr(n)=5 composite only n=6
     вЖТ Proved: F(k)>k for all kвЙ•6 by induction

  в≠Р vвВВ(n!)+vвВГ(n!) = n вЯЇ {4,6} вАФ p-adic factorial #161
     вЖТ Legendre: vвВВ(6!)=4, vвВГ(6!)=2, sum=6 вЬУ
     вЖТ Condition: n = sвВГ(n)+2¬ЈsвВВ(n) (digit sum equation)
     вЖТ Proof: sвВГ(n)+2sвВВ(n) вЙ§ O(log n) вЙ™ n for large n, finitely many
     вЖТ Verified unique pair to n=100000. 6 is the larger solution

  в≠Р max{n : ѕЖ(ѕЖ(n))=1} = 6 вАФ largest 1-primitive-root number #162
     вЖТ ѕЖ(ѕЖ(n))=1 вЯЇ ѕЖ(n)вИИ{1,2} вЯЇ nвИИ{1,2,3,4,6}

### Riemann Hypothesis Connection Details

```
  ѕГвВЛвВБ(n) = ѕГ(n)/n average = ѕА¬≤/6 = ќґ(2)  вЖР Riemann
  R(n) = ѕГвВЛвВБ(n) ¬Ј ѕЖ(n)/ѕД(n)
  вЖТ The average behavior of R depends on ќґ(2)

  Riemann Hypothesis вЯє ѕГ(n) < e^ќ≥ ¬Ј n ¬Ј ln(ln(n)) (Robin inequality, nвЙ•5041)
  вЖТ R(n) < e^ќ≥ ¬Ј ln(ln(n)) ¬Ј ѕЖ(n)/ѕД(n)

  Possibility that the gap structure of the R spectrum is related to ќґ zeros:
  - Gap positions = "arithmetic shadows" of ќґ zeros?
  - d_box вЙИ 0.155 = related to Re(s)?? (speculative)
```
